[30;1m242 | [0m[35m## Taking Down Workers[0m
[30;1m243 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m244 | [0m[35mIf, at any time, the worker receives `SIGINT` (via Ctrl+C) or `SIGTERM` (via[0m
[30;1m245 | [0m[35m`kill`), the worker wait until the currently running task is finished, stop[0m
[30;1m246 | [0m[35mthe work loop and gracefully register its own death.[0m
[30;1m247 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m297 | [0m[35m## Time to live for job in queue[0m
[30;1m298 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m299 | [0m[35mA job has two TTLs, one for the job result, `result_ttl`, and one for the job itself, `ttl`.[0m
[30;1m300 | [0m[35mThe latter is used if you have a job that shouldn't be executed after a certain amount of time.[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m493[0m[34m of [0m[33m498[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000610[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.LOLBAS.Linux[0m
  Severity: [36mModerate[0m, Confidence: [36mLow[0m
  Filename: [33m/rq-2.3.1/docs/docs/jobs.md[0m
   Pattern: [32m\s(apt|apt\-get|aria2c|arp|ash|awk|base64|bash|bpftrace|busybox|cat|chmod|chown|cp|cpan|cpulimit|crontab|csh|curl|cut|dash|dd|diff|dmesg|dmsetup|dnf|docker|dpkg|easy_install|ed|emacs|env|expand|expect|facter|find|finger|flock|fmt|ftp|gawk|gdb|gimp|git|grep|head|iftop|ionice|ip|irb|jjs|journalctl|jrunscript|ksh|ld\.so|ldconfig|logsave|ltrace|lua|mail|mawk|mount|mtr|mv|mysql|nano|nawk|nc|nice|nl|nmap|node|od|openssl|perl|pg|php|pic|pico|pip|puppet|readelf|red|rlogin|rlwrap|rpm|rpmquery|rsync|ruby|run\-mailcap|run\-parts|rvim|scp|screen|script|sed|service|setarch|sftp|shuf|smbclient|socat|sort|sqlite3|ssh|start\-stop\-daemon|stdbuf|strace|systemctl|tail|tar|taskset|tclsh|tcpdump|tee|telnet|tftp|time|timeout|tmux|top|ul|unexpand|uniq|unshare|vi|vim|watch|wget|whois|wish|xargs|xxd|yum|zsh|zypper)\s[0m
[30;1m85 | [0m[35m  (e.g. `'1h'`, `'3m'`, `'5s'`).[0m
[30;1m86 | [0m[35m* `result_ttl` specifies how long (in seconds) successful jobs and their[0m
[30;1m87 | [0m[35m  results are kept. Expired jobs will be automatically deleted. Defaults to 500 seconds.[0m
[30;1m88 | [0m[35m* `ttl` specifies the maximum queued time (in seconds) of the job before it's discarded.[0m
[30;1m89 | [0m[35m  This argument defaults to `None` (infinite TTL).[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35m* `failure_ttl` specifies how long (in seconds) failed jobs are kept (defaults to 1 year)[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35m* `depends_on` specifies another job (or job id) that must complete before this[0m

[30;1m24 | [0m[35m## Testing on Windows[0m
[30;1m25 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m26 | [0m[35mIf you are testing on a Windows machine you can use the approach above, but with a slight tweak.[0m
[30;1m27 | [0m[35mYou will need to subclass SimpleWorker to override the default timeout mechanism of the worker.[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35mReason: Windows OS does not implement some underlying signals utilized by the default SimpleWorker.[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35mTo subclass SimpleWorker for Windows you can do the following:[0m
